----LTE reselect to GSM
/////////////
Note:
measurement object
	ARFCN(GSM cell information in SIB7)
measurement timing
	After decoding the paging,UE could do GSM cell measurement until next paging occasion
Three tasks
	RSSI  measurement
	Initial BSIC identification
		BSIC=BCC+NCC
		BSC is GSM Physical Cell ID to uniquely identify different cell using same frequency
	BSIC reconfirmation
		Once a GSM cell has been identified,BSIC shall be reconfirmed

***********************************************************************************
*********************************special case**************************************
***********************************************************************************

----1. stuck in 3G issue:

(1). Why UE camped on 3G.
The silent log is caught late. so the CP only record that UE camp on 3G cell and then register on it.
and as UE is set as 2g/3g/4g auto, it's normal that UE camp on 3G according to the signal situation.

 

(2). After UE camped on 3G, it should measure whether it need to reselect to 4G.

//re-dial
  We will redial the call if the DisconnectCause is not the below:
        if (((mPreviousGsmCallState == Call.State.DIALING) || (mPreviousGsmCallState == Call.State.ALERTING))
                && (PhoneFeature.hasFeature(PhoneFeature.FEATURE_MULTISIM) ? (!MultiSimPhoneNumberUtils
                        .isEmergencyNumber(number)) : (!PhoneNumberUtils.isEmergencyNumber(number)))
                && (cause != Connection.DisconnectCause.INCOMING_MISSED)
                && (cause != Connection.DisconnectCause.NORMAL)
                && (cause != Connection.DisconnectCause.LOCAL)
                && (cause != Connection.DisconnectCause.INCOMING_REJECTED)
                && (cause != Connection.DisconnectCause.FDN_BLOCKED)
                && (cause != Connection.DisconnectCause.INVALID_NUMBER)
                && (cause != Connection.DisconnectCause.ERROR_UNSPECIFIED)

	typedef enum
	{
	  /** @cond
	  */
	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_NONE = -1,   /* FOR INTERNAL USE OF CM ONLY! */
	  /** @endcond
	  */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_PWROFF = 0,
		/**< Phone is powering off. */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_FTM = 1,
		/**< Phone is in factory test mode. */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_OFFLINE = 2,
		/**< Phone is offline. */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_OFFLINE_AMPS = 3,
		/**< Phone is offline analog. */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_OFFLINE_CDMA = 4,
		/**< Phone is offline CDMA. */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_ONLINE = 5,
		/**< Phone is online. */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_LPM = 6,
		/**< Phone is in Low Power Mode (LPM) . */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_RESET = 7,
		/**< Phone is resetting (i.e., power-cycling). */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_NET_TEST_GW = 8,
		/**< Phone is conducting network test for GSM/WCDMA. This mode can
			 <i>not</i> be set by clients. It can only be set by the lower
			 layers of the stack. */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_OFFLINE_IF_NOT_FTM = 9,
		/**< This mode is only set when there is an offline request during
			 power-up. This mode cannot be set by clients. It can
			 only be set by the task mode controller. */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_PSEUDO_ONLINE = 10,
		/**< Phone is pseudo online, transmit disabled. */

	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_RESET_MODEM = 11,
		/**< Phone is resetting the modem processor. */

	  /** @cond
	  */
	  SYS_OPRT_MODE_MAX   /* FOR INTERNAL USE OF CM ONLY! */
	  /** @endcond
	  */

	} sys_oprt_mode_e_type;

*********************************Technical Report**********************************
***********************************************************************************	
To:		北京SW验证
From:		广州三星研究院 SW开发
Date:		7/7/2015
Subject:	 	No network deadlock


[Introduction]
This report provides SRC_GZ R&D’s responses to Samsung Beijing S/W Engineering

[Reported issues and Samsung Responses]
	PLM ISSUE: P150622-00735//表格

	.1	No network deadlock



[Analysis Result] 
	[Problem Description]
	LTE may release TRM chains incorrectly due to which user may not be able to obtain service for a long time.

	[Problem Scenario]
	1) UE in DSDS mode 
	2) loses service while moving from connected to idle mode
	3) Highler layers (NAS/MMODE) to send a service request while LTE is recovering from conneced to idle mode service loss
	4)the failure frequency is rarely


	[ Problem Recovery]
	UE will recover if a PLMN search or another request for service is issued by higher layers.

	[Change Description]
	Changes are made to clear the timers related to the carrier when a pending TRM request is cancelled. This will make sure the timers will not expire leading to LTE incorrectly release the chains and getting stuck in NO service.
	CR772432 fixed this iusse.
	Related files:lte_ml1_rfmgr_trm.c

	[Log analysis]

[Conclusion]




***********************************************************************************
*********************************OTA Detail**********************************
***********************************************************************************
